Roman',serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:700;line-height:120%">Item 3.01 Notice of Delisting or Failure to Satisfy a Continued Listing Rule or Standard; Transfer of Listing.</span></div><div><span><br/></span></div><div style="text-align:justify"><span style="color:#000000;font-family:'Times New Roman',serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">As previously disclosed on that certain Current Report on Form 8-K as filed with the Securities and Exchange Commission on August 27, 2025, on August 27, 2025, CaliberCos Inc. (the &#8220;Company&#8221;) received a notification letter from the Nasdaq Listing Qualifications Staff (the &#8220;Staff&#8221;) of The Nasdaq Stock Market LLC (&#8220;Nasdaq&#8221;) notifying the Company that its amount of stockholders&#8217; equity had fallen below the $2,500,000 required minimum for continued listing set forth in Nasdaq Listing Rule 5550(b)(1) (the &#8220;Listing Rule&#8221;).</span></div><div style="text-align:justify"><span><br/></span></div><div style="text-align:justify"><span style="color:#000000;font-family:'Times New Roman',serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">On November 17, 2025, the Company received a letter from Nasdaq stating that based on the Company&#8217;s Form 10-Q for the period ended September 30, 2025, evidencing stockholders&#8217; equity of $6,087,000, the Staff has determined that the Company has regained compliance with the Listing Rule. Nasdaq has closed the matter.</span></div><div style="text-align:justify"><span><br/></span></div><div id="ic06c9c6ab20d4f3d96ba10ad5f0552ce_10"></div><div><span style="color:#000000;font-family:'Times New Roman',serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:700;line-height:120%">Item 7.01 Regulation FD Disclosure.</span></div><div><span><br/></span></div><div style="text-align:justify"><span style="color:#000000;font-family:'Times New Roman',serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">On November 18, 2025, the Company issued a press release announcing that the Company has regained compliance with the Listing Rule.</span></div><div style="text-align:justify"><span><br/></span></div><div style="text-align:justify"><span style="color:#000000;font-family:'Times New Roman',serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">A copy of the press release is attached to this Current Report on Form 8-K as Exhibit 99.1 and is hereby furnished pursuant to this Item 7.01. </span></div><div style="text-align:justify"><span><br/></span></div><div style="text-align:justify"><span style="color:#000000;font-family:'Times New Roman',serif;font-size:10pt;font-style:italic;font-weight:400;line-height:112%">The information disclosed under this Item 7.01, including Exhibit 99.1 attached hereto, shall not be deemed &#8220;filed&#8221; for purposes of Section 18 of the Securities Exchange Act of 1934, as amended (the &#8220;Exchange Act&#8221;), or deemed incorporated by reference in any filing under the Securities Act of 1933, as amended, or the Exchange Act, except as shall be expressly set forth by specific reference in such a filing.</span></div><div id="ic06c9c6ab20d4f3d96ba10ad5f0552ce_13"></div><div style="-sec-extract:summary;margin-top:12pt"><span style="color:#000000;font-family:'Times New Roman',serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:700;line-height:120%">Item 9.01.
